property	description
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_ctdiPhantomTypeCode	The type of phantom to use for CTDI measurement according to IEC 60601-2-44
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_ctdiVol	The average dose over the total volume scanned for the selected CT conditions of operation (calculated according to IEC 60601-2-44, Ed.2.1 (Clause 29.1.103.4)). The units are energy dose, e.g. mGy.
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_exposureModulationType_Code	The manner in which tube current is varied in order to limit the dose.
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_gantryDetectorTilt	Nominal angle of tilt in degrees of the scanning gantry. The units are of plane angle , e.g. degrees. Zero degrees means the gantry is not tilted, negative degrees are when the top of the gantry is tilted away from where the table enters the gantry.
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_kVp	Peak kilovoltage output of the x-ray generator. The units are of electrical potential.
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_singleCollimationWidth	The width of a single row of acquired data. The units are of linear distance, e.g. mm.
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_spiralPitchFactor	Ratio of the distance that the table moves during a complete revolution of the source around the gantry orbit, to the width of the total collimation over the area of active x-ray detection. The units are of unity.
CTAquisitionProtocolElement_totalCollimationWidth	The width of the total collimation over the area of active x-ray detection. The units are of linear distance, e.g. mm.
CTImageReconstructionProtocolElement_convolutionKernel	A label describing the mathematical operations used to reconstruct images from the acquired data. The values for this attribute are vendor specific and not coded.
CTImageReconstructionProtocolElement_convolutionKernelGroupCode	A coded value specifying the family of mathematical operations to use to reconstruct images from the acquired data
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_acquisitionContrastCode	A coded value specifying the inherent (as opposed to exogenous) contrast in the acquisition.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_arterialSpinLabelingContrastCode	A coded value specifying how arterial water is used as a diffusable tracer.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_diffusionBValue	The factor by which the acquisition is sensitized to the Brownian motion of water molecules. The units are of time/area, e.g. s/mm2
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_diffusionDirectionalityCode	A coded value specifying whether diffusion conditions for the frame are directional, or isotropic with respect to direction
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_echoPlanarPulseSequenceIndicator	Specifies whether multiple echos of different phase steps are acquired using rephasing gradients instead of repeated 180-degree pulses.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_echoPulseSequenceCategoryCode	A coded value specifying an echo category of pulse sequences.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_inversionRecoveryIndicator	Specifies whether an inversion recovery preparatory sequence is used in the acquisition.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_magneticFieldStrength	A vector quantity indicating the ability of a magnetic field to exert a force on moving electric charges. [The American Heritage Science Dictionary]. The units are of magnetic flux density, e.g. tesla.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_multipleSpinEchoIndicator	Specifies whether different lines in k-space are collected for a single frame.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_phaseContrastIndicator	Specifies whether this is a pulse sequence in which the flowing spins are velocity encoded in phase.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_pulseSequenceName	Name of the pulse sequence that is used for the acquisition. This is usually a vendor-specific name.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_resonantNucleusCode	A coded value specifying the atomic nucleus that is the target of the acquisition
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_saturationRecoveryIndicator	Specifies whether a saturation recovery pulse sequence is used
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_spectrallySelectedSuppressionCode	A coded value specifying the type of substance-specific signal suppression is used.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_steadyStatePulseSequenceCode	A coded value specifying how residual transverse magnetization is maintained during the acquisition.
MRImageAcquisitionProtocolElement_timeOfFlightContrastIndicator	Specifies whether contrast is created by the inflow of blood in the saturated plane.
MRImageReconstructionProtocolElement_complexImageComponentCode	A coded value specifying the channel of the quadrature detected data, or the combination derived from those channels, used to reconstruct the image
MultiplexMicroscopy_id	MultiplexMicroscopy identifier
NonDICOMCTimages_id	NonDICOMCTimages identifier
NonDICOMMRimages_id	NonDICOMMRimages identifier
NonDICOMPETimages_id	NonDICOMPETimages identifier
NonDICOMpathologyImages_id	NonDICOMpathologyImages identifier
NonDICOMradiologyAllModalities_id	NonDICOMradiologyAllModalities identifier
PETImagingAcquisitionProtocolElement_gantryDetectorTilt	Nominal angle of tilt in degrees of the scanning gantry. The units are of plane angle , e.g. degrees. Zero degrees means the gantry is not tilted, negative degrees are when the top of the gantry is tilted away from where the table enters the gantry.
Radiopharmaceutical_radionuclideCode	A coded value that specifies the radioactive isotope in the radiophamaceutical.
acl	open or restricted access to data
acquisition_method_type	Records the method of acquisition or source for the specimen under consideration
adult_or_childhood_study	Study participants are adult, pediatric, or other
age_at_diagnosis	Participant age at relevant diagnosis
aliquot_id	One or more characters used to identify a portion of a sample.
analytical_fractions	The portion of a specimen that was isolated from the whole and collected via a fractionation process to be subjected to further analysis.
antibody_name	short descriptive name for this antibody
authz	multifactor authorization
avg_read_length	Average sequence read length
bases	Total number of unique bases read
bioproject_accession	NCBI BioProject accession ID
biosample_accession	NCBI BioSample accession ID (SAMN) for this sample
catalog_number	catalog number from vendor
cds_primary_bucket	The primary bucket for depositing data
cds_requestor	Identifies the user requesting storage in CDS
cds_secondary_bucket	Secondary bucket for depositing data (non-sequence files)
cds_tertiary_bucket	Secondary bucket for depositing data (non-sequence files)
channel_id	The unique channel identifier for each channel in this image must match the corresponding field in the OME-TIFF header
channel_metadata_filename	File name of uploaded companion CSV file containing channel-level metadata details
channel_name	Channel label for each channel in this image must match the corresponding field in the OME-TIFF header
checksum_algorithm	The method by which the file checksum was calculated.
checksum_value	checksum (hash) for file (using checksum_algorithm) - if you want to use a checksum other than md5
citation_or_DOI	Publication and/or digital object identifier of the publication for open access studies
